msg:Let's talk about the hotel environment and facilities first. The hotel is in the forest park. The surrounding environment is very good and quiet. It is convenient to walk around and has high negative oxygen ions. There is a large public rest space in the hotel lobby where you can read books, drink coffee and tea. We lived in a log cabin. The room supplies were clean and complete. Earplugs and eye masks were also prepared thoughtfully. The structure design of the house was convenient for use. There was floor heating and it was not cold in winter.

Let's talk about the service. The staff took the initiative to add WeChat to communicate the needs before arriving at the store, and greeted us at the door of the manor. There were welcome fruits and yogurt. Because it was the off-season, there were not many staff, but the service responded very quickly, and they greeted us actively and warmly. Not only did they provide a lot of travel suggestions, but they also took us to the park to find squirrels. The service was really attentive and received six-star praise.

There were not many dining options, only breakfast, and you could also go to the town to solve it.

In general, it was much more satisfactory than other hotels I had stayed in along the way in Yili. It was the first choice for traveling to Nalati.
